URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS224387490	2019-01-05 00:02:26	31943	species	White-throated Sparrow	Zonotrichia albicollis			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Churchill	US-NV-001	US-NV_973	9			Carson River Diversion Dam	L421280	H	39.4919804	-118.9933405	2014-01-02	13:25:00	obsr404509	S16191452	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	65	1.127		2	1		0	1	1		Drove and walked the road on the south side of the dam and then .5 miles east on Pioneer rd.	Either a Tan-striped of 1st year White-throated sparrow was found along the edge of a moderitly brushy area with some cottonwood, elm and Russian Olive trees close by. It was fairly shy but appeared and sat a couple of times on the edge of a Russian Olive tree for good looks from 15 to 30 feet. Viewed with the naked eye and through 10x42 glasses. The day was clear and sunny in the afternoon. Overall it appeared to be just a tad smaller than the White-crowned sparrows that were nearby. It also appeared to have a lighter whitish belly and an obvious white-throat outlined by grayish cheeks and very light brownish/grayish streaked chest. It also showed a yellowish strip in front of the eye extending from the bill to just about mid-eye, above the eye. From mid-eye this eye-brow strip turns white to whiteish/lt. brownish and extends to the back of the head. There is also a dark brown stripe that extends from the middle of the eye--under the white--to the back of the head. And darkish brown crown stripes with a lighter middle of the head stripe. The bill itself is darkish gray. Was able to get a very good side view photo that is available by return e-mail.
